Attempting to run on a sm \",\n   302→          dprops->major,\n   303→          \".\",\n   304→          dprops->minor,\n   305→          \" gpu.\");\n   306→    }\n   307→    return false;\n   308→  }\n   309→#endif\n   310→  return true;\n   311→}\n   312→\n   313→bool check_mem_efficient_hardware_support(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   314→  // Mem Efficient attention supports hardware in the range [sm_50, sm_90]\n   315→  using sm50 = SMVersion<5, 0>;\n   316→  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n   317→#if USE_ROCM\n   318→#if USE_ROCM_ATTENTION\n   319→  if(at::globalContext().getROCmFAPreferredBackend() == at::ROCmFABackend::Ck) {\n   320→    // User explicitly set CK as the flash attention backend. Return true for now\n   321→    // TODO: Flesh out sanity checks\n   322→    return true;\n   323→  } else {\n   324→    auto stream = at::cuda::getCurrentCUDAStream().stream();\n   325→    if (hipSuccess != aotriton::v2::flash::check_gpu(stream)) {\n   326→        auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n   327→        if (debug) {\n   328→            TORCH_WARN(\n   329→                    \"Mem Efficient attention was not compiled for current AMD GPU architecture. Attempting to run on architecture \", dprops->gcnArchName);\n   330→        }\n   331→        return false;\n   332→    }\n   333→#if AOTRITON_VERSION_MINOR >= 9\n   334→    if (aotriton::isArchExperimentallySupported(stream)) {\n   335→      static const bool enable_experimental = c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_ROCM_AOTRITON_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL\") == true;\n   336→      if (!enable_experimental) {\n   337→        TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"Mem Efficient attention on Current AMD GPU is still experimental.\"\n   338→            \" Enable it with TORCH_ROCM_AOTRITON_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL=1.\");\n   339→        return false;\n   340→      }\n   341→    }\n   342→#endif\n   343→  }\n   344→#else\n   345→  return false;\n   346→#endif\n   347→#else\n   348→  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n   349→  if (!check_sm_version<sm50, sm121>(dprops)) {\n   350→    if (debug) {\n   351→      TORCH_WARN(\n   352→          \"Mem Efficient Attention only supports gpu architectures in the range [sm50, sm121]. Attempting to run on a sm \",\n   353→          dprops->major,\n   354→          \".\",\n   355→          dprops->minor,\n   356→          \" gpu.\");\n   357→    }\n   358→    return false;\n   359→  }\n   360→#endif\n   361→  return true;\n   362→}\n   363→\n   364→bool check_requires_grad_and_head_dim_gt192_constraints_on_sm86_89_or_120(\n   365→    sdp_params const& params,\n   366→    bool debug) {\n   367→  // Flash Attention will raise an error in the backward pass if the head_dim\n   368→  // size is greater than 192 And the device is between in the range [sm86, sm89]\n   369→  using sm86 = SMVersion<8, 6>;\n   370→  using sm89 = SMVersion<8, 9>;\n   371→  using sm120 = SMVersion<12, 0>;\n   372→  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n   373→  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n   374→  bool is_sm86_or_sm89 = check_sm_version<sm86, sm89>(dprops);\n   375→  bool is_sm120_or_sm121 = check_sm_version<sm120, sm121>(dprops);\n   376→  bool is_head_dim_gt192 = params.query.sym_size(-1) > 192;\n   377→  bool is_head_dim_lte224 = params.query.sym_size(-1) <= 224;\n   378→  bool is_dropout = params.dropout > 0.0;\n   379→  //  head_dim size  in (192, 224] is not supported on sm86 and sm89\n   380→  bool cond1 = is_head_dim_gt192 && is_head_dim_lte224;\n   381→  // head_dim size > 224 and is_dropout is not supported on sm86 and sm89\n   382→  bool cond2 = params.query.sym_size(-1) > 224 && is_dropout;\n   383→  if (input_requires_grad(params) && (is_sm86_or_sm89 || is_sm120_or_sm121) && (cond1 || cond2)) {\n   384→    if (debug) {\n   385→      TORCH_WARN(\n   386→          \"Flash attention currently doesn't support training with head_dim ∈ (192, 224] or \"\n   387→          \"(head_dim ∈ (224, 256] and dropout > 0.0) on gpu architectures in the range[sm86, sm89].\",\n   388→          \"Attempting to run with dropout set to: \", params.dropout,\n   389→          \"and head_dim: \",\n   390→          params.query.sym_size(-1), \" on a sm \", dprops->major, \".\",\n   391→          dprops->minor, \" gpu.\");\n   392→    }\n   393→    return false;\n   394→  }\n   395→  return true;\n   396→}\n   397→\n   398→bool check_flash_causal_non_square_seqlens(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   399→  // FlashAttention 2 updated the default mask meaning for causal in this PR:\n   400→  // 9e5e8bc91e it is now aligned to lower_right which would be a BC break\n   401→  // for non-square masks. We will not support non-square masks for causal w/ FAV2\n   402→  if (params.is_causal &&\n   403→      !params.query.is_nested() && !params.key.is_nested() &&\n   404→      params.query.sym_size(-2) != params.key.sym_size(-2)) {\n   405→    if (debug) {\n   406→      TORCH_WARN(\n   407→          \"Flash attention does not support the is_causal flag when seqlen_q != seqlen_k. \",\n   408→          \"Got seqlen_q: \", params.query.sym_size(-2), \" seqlen_k: \",\n   409→          params.key.sym_size(-2), \". If you would like to use causal attention with non-square masks, please see CausalAttnMask.\");\n   410→    }\n   411→    return false;\n   412→  }\n   413→  return true;\n   414→}\n   415→\n   416→bool check_all_tensors_on_device(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   417→  // Check that all tensors are on the GPU device\n   418→  // This should be handled by the stub dispatch, but we call can_use_*_attention\n   419→  // directly from python we need to ensure that the tensors are on cuda\n   420→  if (params.query.device().type() != at::DeviceType::CUDA) {\n   421→    if (debug) {\n   422→      TORCH_WARN(\n   423→          \"All tensors need to be on cuda device. Got query on device: \",\n   424→          params.query.device(),\n   425→          \", key on device: \",\n   426→          params.key.device(),\n   427→          \", value on device: \",\n   428→          params.value.device());\n   429→    }\n   430→    return false;\n   431→  }\n   432→  return true;\n   433→}\n   434→\n   435→bool check_cudnn_tensor_shapes(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   436→  const auto s_q = params.query.sym_size(2);\n   437→  const auto s_k = params.key.sym_size(2);\n   438→  const auto d_qk = params.query.sym_size(3);\n   439→  const auto d_v = params.value.sym_size(3);\n   440→  long cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();\n   441→  if (cudnn_version < 8903) {\n   442→    if (debug) {\n   443→      TORCH_WARN(\"SDPA fprop requires cudnn 8.9.3 or higher\");\n   444→    }\n   445→    return false;\n   446→  }\n   447→  if (cudnn_version < 8906 && params.dropout != 0.0) {\n   448→    if (debug) {\n   449→      TORCH_WARN(\"Dropout reference is only supported on 8.9.6 onwards.\");\n   450→    }\n   451→    return false;\n   452→  }\n   453→  auto head_dim_limit = 128;\n   454→  if (cudnn_version >= 91000) {\n   455→    auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n   456→    if (dprops->major == 9 && !dprops->minor) {\n   457→      head_dim_limit = 256;\n   458→    }\n   459→  }\n   460→  if (d_qk > head_dim_limit || d_v > head_dim_limit) {\n   461→    if (debug) {\n   462→      TORCH_WARN(\"head_dim should be no more than \", head_dim_limit);\n   463→    }\n   464→    return false;\n   465→  }\n   466→  if (d_qk % 8 != 0 || d_v % 8 != 0) {\n   467→    if (debug) {\n   468→      TORCH_WARN(\"head_dim should be a multiple of 8\");\n   469→    }\n   470→    return false;\n   471→  }\n   472→  if (cudnn_version < 8906 && s_k % 64 != 0 ) {\n   473→    if (debug) {\n   474→      TORCH_WARN(\"not-multiple-of-64 seq_kv is not supported below 8.9.6\");\n   475→    }\n   476→    return false;\n   477→  }\n   478→  if (cudnn_version < 90000) {\n   479→    if (s_q < 64) {\n   480→      if (debug) {\n   481→        TORCH_WARN(\"s_q less than 64 is not supported before cudnn 9.0.0\");\n   482→      }\n   483→      return false;\n   484→    }\n   485→    if (params.dropout != 0.0 && (s_q % 64 != 0 || s_k % 64 != 0)) {\n   486→      if (debug) {\n   487→        TORCH_WARN(\n   488→            \"s_q not a multiple of 64 with padding/dropout is not supported with cudnn version 9.0.0\");\n   489→      }\n   490→      return false;\n   491→    }\n   492→  }\n   493→  if (s_k == 1) {\n   494→    if (debug) {\n   495→      TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"cudnn SDPA does not support key/value sequence length 1.\");\n   496→    }\n   497→    return false;\n   498→  }\n   499→ return false;\n   504→  }\n   505→  return true;\n   506→}\n   507→\n   508→bool check_cudnn_layout(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   509→  const int64_t h = params.query.size(1);\n   510→  const int64_t s_q = params.query.size(2);\n   511→  const int64_t d = params.query.size(3);\n   512→  const int64_t s_k = params.key.size(2);\n   513→  const int64_t s_v = params.value.size(2);\n   514→  // corresponds to cuDNN's \"packed QKV\" layout\n   515→  const bool packed_query_layout_ok = (params.query.stride(0) == s_q * 3 * h * d) &&\n   516→                                 (params.query.stride(1) == d) &&\n   517→                                 (params.query.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n   518→                                 (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n   519→  const bool packed_key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * 3 * h * d) &&\n   520→                               (params.key.stride(1) == d) &&\n   521→                               (params.key.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n   522→                               (params.key.stride(3) == 1);\n   523→  const bool packed_value_layout_ok = (params.value.stride(0) == s_v * 3 * h * d) &&\n   524→                                 (params.value.stride(1) == d) &&\n   525→                                 (params.value.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n   526→                                 (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n   527→\n   528→  const bool packed_layout_ok = packed_query_layout_ok && packed_key_layout_ok && packed_value_layout_ok;\n   529→\n   530→  const bool query_layout_ok = (params.query.stride(0) == s_q * h * d) &&\n   531→                               (params.query.stride(1) == d) &&\n   532→                               (params.query.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n   533→                               (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n   534→  const bool key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * h * d) &&\n   535→                              (params.key.stride(1) == d) &&\n   536→                              (params.key.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n   537→                              (params.key.stride(3) == 1);\n   538→  const bool value_layout_ok = (params.value.stride(0) == s_v * h * d) &&\n   539→                               (params.value.stride(1) == d) &&\n   540→                               (params.value.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n   541→                               (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n   542→\n   543→  const bool layout_ok = query_layout_ok && key_layout_ok && value_layout_ok;\n   544→\n   545→  if (!packed_value_layout_ok && !layout_ok) {\n   546→    if (debug) {\n   547→      if (!packed_layout_ok) {\n   548→        if (!packed_query_layout_ok) {\n   549→          TORCH_WARN(\"Query tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.query.strides());\n   550→        }\n   551→        if (!packed_key_layout_ok) {\n   552→          TORCH_WARN(\"Key tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.key.strides());\n   553→        }\n   554→        if (!packed_value_layout_ok) {\n   555→          TORCH_WARN(\"Value tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.value.strides());\n   556→        }\n   557→      }\n   558→      if (!layout_ok) {\n   559→        if (!query_layout_ok) {\n   560→          TORCH_WARN(\"Query tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.query.strides());\n   561→        }\n   562→        if (!key_layout_ok) {\n   563→          TORCH_WARN(\"Key tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.key.strides());\n   564→        }\n   565→        if (!value_layout_ok) {\n   566→          TORCH_WARN(\"Value tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.value.strides());\n   567→        }\n   568→      }\n   569→    }\n   570→    return false;\n   571→  }\n   572→  return true;\n   573→}\n   574→\n   575→bool check_cudnn_hardware_support(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   576→  using sm80 = SMVersion<8, 0>;\n   577→  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n   578→  auto dprops =  657→bool can_use_cudnn_attention(const sdp_params& params, bool debug) {\n   658→#if defined(USE_ROCM) || !AT_CUDNN_ENABLED() || !defined(CUDNN_VERSION)\n   659→  if (debug) {\n   660→ 666→    TORCH_WARN(CUDNN_VERSION, \" cuDNN version too old to use cuDNN Attention (< v9.0.0)\");\n   667→  }\n   668→  return false;\n   669→#endif\n   670→#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION)\n   671→  static auto cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();\n   672→  if (params.dropout > 0.0 && cudnn_version > 91100 && cudnn_version < 91400) {\n   673→    if (debug) {\n   674→ that determine if a flash kernel can be ran\n   680→  // Replace with std::to_array when we migrate to c++20\n   681→  constexpr auto general_constraints =\n   682→      c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(\n   683→          check_runtime_disabled_cudnn,\n   684→          check_for_nested_inputs,\n   685→          check_all_tensors_on_device,\n   686→          check_tensor_shapes,\n   687→          check_cudnn_deterministic,\n   688→          check_dtypes_low_precision,\n   689→          check_attn_mask_shape,\n   690→          check_cudnn_hardware_support\n   691→          );\n   692→  for (auto& constraint : general_constraints) {\n   693→    if (!constraint(params, debug)) {\n   694→      return false;\n   695→    }\n   696→  }\n   697→  constexpr auto dense_constraints =\n   698→      c10::array_of<bool (*)(sdp_params const&, bool)>(\n   699→      check_nonzero_sequence_lengths_dense,\n   700→      check_last_dim_stride_equals_1_dense<true /*ignore_singleton_dim=*/>,\n   701→      check_batch_size_and_num_heads_dense<true /*enable_gqa*/, false /*requires_same_num_heads*/>,\n   702→      check_cudnn_tensor_shapes\n   703→  );\n   704→\n   705→  if (has_only_dense_inputs(params)) {\n   706→    for (auto& constraint : dense_constraints) {\n   707→      if (!constraint(params, debug)) {\n   708→        return false;\n   709→      }\n   710→    }\n   711→  }\n   712→  return true;\n   713→}\n   714→\n   715→bool is_flash_attention_available() {\n   716→#ifdef USE_FLASH_ATTENTION\n   717→  return true;\n   718→#else\n   719→  return false;\n   720→#endif\n   721→}\n   722→\n   723→bool can_use_flash_attention(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   724→#ifndef 775→bool can_use_mem_efficient_attention(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   776→#ifndef USE_MEM_EFF_ATTENTION\n   777→  TORCH_WARN_ONCE(!debug, \"Torch was not compiled with memory efficient check_requires_grad_and_head_dim_gt192_constraints_on_sm86_89_or_120(\n    sdp_params const& params,\n    bool debug) {\n  // Flash Attention will raise an error in the backward pass if the head_dim\n In a backwards, you knew what\n   358→// the original size of the input tensor was, so you can cache that\n   359→// geometry and fill it directly. Conv_v8.cpp contains implementation\n// with v8 API.\n//\n// NOTE [ Convolution design ]\n//\n// cuDNN convolutions does not handle bias. (OTOH: We can always pass in\n// grad_input/grad_output, so this is not very pressing)\nvoid setConvolutionParams(\n    ConvolutionParams* params,\n    const at::Tensor& input,\n    const at::Tensor& ArrayRef<int>(params.stride, dim - 2) << \", \";\n  ss << \"dilation=\" << ArrayRef<int>(params.dilation, dim - 2) << \", \";\n  ss << \"groups=\" << params.groups << \")\\n\";\n  ss << \"net = net.cuda().\" << partial_dtype << \"()\" << to_channels_last\n     << \"\\n\";\n  ss << \"out = net(data)\\n\";\n  ss << \"out.backward(torch.randn_like(out))\\n\";\n  ss << \"torch.cuda.synchronize()\\n\\n\";\n\n  return ss.str();\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n//\n// Convolution forward / Transposed convolution backward\n//\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nvoid cudnn_convolution_forward_out(\n    TensorArg& output,\n    CheckedFrom c,\n    const TensorArg& input,\n    const TensorArg& weight,\n    IntArrayRef padding,\n    IntArrayRef stride,\n    IntArrayRef dilation,\n    int64_t groups,\n    bool benchmark,\n    bool deterministic,\n    bool allow_tf32) {\n  checkAllSameType(c, {input, weight});\n  checkAllSameGPU(c, {input, weight});\n\n  auto memory_format = output->suggest_memory_format();\n  convolution_shape_check(\n      c, input, weight, output, padding, stride, dilation, groups);\n\n  Tensor weight_contig = weight->contiguous(memory_format);\n  Tensor input_contig = input->contiguous(memory_format);\n\n  raw_cudnn_convolution_forward_out(\n      *output,\n      input_contig,\n      weight_contig,\n      padding,\n      stride,\n      dilation,\n      groups,\n      benchmark,\n      deterministic,\n      allow_tf32);\n}\n\nTensor cudnn_convolution(\n    const Tensor& input_t,\n    const Tensor& weight_t,\n    IntArrayRef padding,\n    IntArrayRef stride,\n    IntArrayRef dilation,\n    int64_t groups,\n    bool benchmark,\n    bool deterministic,\n    bool allow_tf32) {\n  TensorArg input{input_t, \"input\", 1}, weight{weight_t, \"weight\", 2};\n  CheckedFrom c = \"cudnn_convolution\";\n  auto memory_format = cudnn_conv_suggest_memory_format(input_t, weight_t);\n  Tensor output_t = at::detail::empty_cuda(\n      conv_output_size(\n          input_t.sizes(), weight_t.sizes(), padding, stride, dilation),\n      input->options().memory_format(memory_format));\n  if (output_t.numel() == 0) {\n    return output_t;\n  }\n  // Avoid ambiguity of \"output\" when this is being used as backwards\n  TensorArg output{output_t, \"result\", 0};\n  cudnn_convolution_forward_out(\n      output,\n      c,\n      input,\n      weight,\n      padding,\n      stride,\n      dilation,\n      groups,\n      benchmark,\n      deterministic,\n      allow_tf32);\n  return *output;\n}\nat::Tensor& cudnn_convolution_out(\n    const Tensor& input_t,\n    const Tensor& weight_t,\n    IntArrayRef padding,\n    IntArrayRef stride,\n    IntArrayRef dilation,\n    int64_t groups,\n    bool benchmark,\n    bool deterministic,\n    bool allow_tf32,\n    Tensor& output_t) {\n  TensorArg input{input_t, \"input\", 1}, weight{weight_t, \"weight\", 2};\n  CheckedFrom c = \"cudnn_convolution\";\n  if (output_t.numel() == 0) {\n    return output_t;\n  }\n  TensorArg output{output_t, \"result\", 0};\n  cudnn_convolution_forward_out(\n      output,\n      c,\n      input,\n      weight,\n      padding,\n      stride,\n      dilation,\n      groups,\n      benchmark,\n      deterministic,\n      allow_tf32);\n  return output_t;\n}\n\n// NB: output_padding not needed here, as there is no ambiguity to resolve\nTensor cudnn_convolution_transpose_backward_input(\n    const Tensor& grad_output_t,\n    const Tensor& weight_t,\n    IntArrayRef padding,\n    IntArrayRef stride,\n    IntArrayRef dilation,\n    int64_t groups,\n    bool benchmark,\n    bool deterministic,\n    bool allow_tf32) {\n  TensorArg grad_output{grad_output_t, \"grad_output\", 1},\n      weight{weight_t, \"weight\", 2};\n  auto memory_format =\n      cudnn_conv_suggest_memory_format(grad_output_t,   output,\n      \"cudnn_convolution_transpose_backward_input\",\n      grad_output,\n      weight,\n      padding,\n      stride,\n      dilation,\n      groups,\n      benchmark,\n      deterministic,\n      allow_tf32);\n  return *output;\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n//\n// Convolution backward / Transposed convolution forward\n//\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n// NOTE [ Backward vs transpose convolutions ]\n//\n// Backward and transpose are algorithmically equivalent, but they\n// compute their geometry differently.  In a backwards, you knew what\n// the original size of the input tensor was, so you can cache that\n// geometry and fill it directly.  In transposed convolution, it is\n// more conventional to not explicitly specify the output (previously\n// input) size, and compute it.  This, however, leaves a degree of\n// freedom; this degree of freedom is resolved using the\n// output_padding parameter.  Both of these interfaces are equivalent,\n// but they are differently convenient depending on the use case.\n\nTensor cudnn_convolution_backward_input(\n    CheckedFrom c,\n    IntArrayRef input_size,\n    const TensorArg& grad_output,\n    const TensorArg& weight,\n    IntArrayRef padding,\n    IntArrayRef stride,\n    IntArrayRef dilation,\n    int64_t groups,\n    bool benchmark,\n    bool deterministic,\n    bool allow_tf32) {\n  checkAllSameType(c, {grad_output, weight});\n  checkAllSameGPU(c, {grad_output, weight});\n\n  auto memory_format = cudnn_conv_suggest_memory_format(*grad_output, *weight);\n  Tensor grad_input_t = at::detail::empty_cuda(\n      input_size, grad_output->options().memory_format(memory_format));\n\n  // Avoid \"grad_input\" when this is being used as transposed convolution\n  TensorArg grad_input{grad_input_t, \"result\", 0};\n  convolution_shape_check(\n      c, grad_input, weight, grad_output, padding, stride, dilation, groups);\n\n  Tensor weight_contig = weight->contiguous(memory_format);\n  Tensor grad_output_contig = grad_output->contiguous(memory_format);\n\n  raw_cudnn_convolution_backward_input_out(\n      *grad_input,\n      grad_output_contig,\n      weight_contig,\n      padding,\n      stride,\n      dilation,\n      groups,\n      benchmark,\n      deterministic,\n      allow_tf32);\n\n  return *grad_input;\n}\n\nTensor cudnn_convolution_transpose_forward(\n    CheckedFrom c,\n    const TensorArg& grad_output,\n    const TensorArg& weight,\n    IntArrayRef padding,\n    IntArrayRef output_padding,\n    IntArrayRef stride,\n    IntArrayRef dilation,\n    int64_t groups,\n    bool benchmark,\n    bool deterministic,\n    bool allow_tf32) {\n  auto input_size = conv_input_size(\n      grad_output->sizes(),\n      weight->sizes(),\n      padding,\n      output_padding,\n      stride,\n      dilation,\n      groups);\n  return deterministic,\n    bool allow_tf32) {\n  TensorArg input{input_t, \"input\", 1}, weight{weight_t, \"weight\", 2};\n  CheckedFrom c = \"cudnn_convolution_transpose\";\n  auto output_t = deterministic,\n      allow_tf32);\n  return output_t;\n}\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n//\n// Convolution backward (weight)\n//\n//    const Tensor& input_t,\n    IntArrayRef padding,\n    IntArrayRef stride,\n    IntArrayRef dilation,\n    int64_t groups,\n    bool benchmark,\n    bool deterministic,\n    bool allow_tf32) {\n  auto layout = cudnn_conv_suggest_memory_format(input_t, grad_output_t);\n\n  Tensor grad_output_contig_t = grad_output_t.contiguous(layout);\n  TensorArg grad_output_contig{grad_output_contig_t, \"grad_output\", 1};\n\n  Tensor input_contig_t = input_t.contiguous(layout);\n  TensorArg input{input_contig_t, \"input\", 2};\n\n  checkAllSameType(c, {grad_output_contig, input});\n cudnn_convolution_backward(\n    const at::Tensor& input,\n    const at::Tensor& grad_output_t,\n    const at::Tensor& weight,\n    IntArrayRef padding,\n    IntArrayRef stride,\n    IntArrayRef include sm86/89\n    77→// Needs to be kept in-sync with test_fused_chocie in test_transformers.py\n    78→bool check_prefer_cudnn_attention() {\n    79→  static const bool prefer_cudnn = c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_PREFERRED\") != false;\n    80→  if (!prefer_cudnn) {\n    81→    return false;\n    82→  }\n    83→#if (defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && (CUDNN_VERSION >= 90900))\n    84→  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n    85→  auto major = dprops->major;\n    86→  return (major == 9 || major == 10) && !dprops->minor;\n    87→#else\n    88→  return false;\n    89→#endif\n    90→}\n    91→\n    92→// flash_attention V2 is universally faster than efficient_attention and Math\n    93→std::array<SDPBackend, num_backends> priority_order(sdp_params const& params) {\n    94→  if (!priority_order_init_) {\n    95→    priority_order_init_ = true;\n    96→    if (check_prefer_cudnn_attention()) {\n    97→        const std::vector<int64_t>                                         static_cast<int64_t>(at::SDPBackend::efficient_attention),\n   100→  105→}\n   106→\n   107→bool use_tensor_cores(sdp_params const& params, cudaDeviceProp* dprops, bool is_half) {\n   108→  if (dprops->major >= 8) {\n   109→    return true;\n   110→  }\n   111→  if (dprops->major >= 7) {\n   112→    return is_half;\n   113→  }\n   114→  return false;\n   115→}\n   116→int64_t minimum_gemm_alignment(sdp_params const& params) {\n   117→  auto dprops =   130→}\n   131→\n   132→// On ROCM, ME and FA share the backend, and hence they share the checking\n   133→// function for fundamental limitations by the GPU kernel\n   134→// caller_is_meff is added 183→template<bool caller_is_meff = false>\n   184→bool check_head_dim_size_flash_nested(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   185→  const auto max_size = c10::SymInt(256);\n   186→  const auto     \" instead.\");\n   230→    }\n   231→    return false;\n   232→  }\n   233→  return true;\n   234→}\n   235→\n   236→template <int Major, int Minor>\n   237→struct SMVersion {\n   238→  static constexpr int major = Major;\n   239→  static constexpr int minor = Minor;\n   240→  constexpr SMVersion() = default;\n   241→};\n   242→\n   243→/**\n   244→ * Checks if the current CUDA device architecture is inclusively within the specified range.\n   245→ *\n   246→ * @param lower_bound The lower bound of the CUDA device architecture range.\n   247→ * @param upper_bound The upper bound of the CUDA device architecture range.\n   248→ * @param params The parameters for the current operation.\n   249→ * @return True if the current CUDA device architecture is within the specified range, false otherwise.\n   250→ */\n   251→template <typename lower_bound, typename upper_bound>\n   252→bool check_sm_version(cudaDeviceProp * dprops) {\n   253→  bool is_gte_lower_bound = dprops->major > lower_bound::major ||\n   254→      (dprops->major == lower_bound::major &&\n   255→       dprops->minor >= lower_bound::minor);\n   256→  bool is_lte_upper_bound = dprops->major < upper_bound::major ||\n   257→      (dprops->major == upper_bound::major &&\n   258→       dprops->minor <= upper_bound::minor);\n   259→  return is_gte_lower_bound && is_lte_upper_bound;\n   260→}\n   261→\n   262→bool check_flash_attention_hardware_support(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   263→  // Check that the gpu is capable of running flash attention\n   264→  using sm80 = SMVersion<8, 0>;\n   265→  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n   266→#if USE_ROCM\n   267→#if USE_ROCM_ATTENTION\n   268→  if(at::globalContext().getROCmFAPreferredBackend() == at::ROCmFABackend::Ck) {\n   269→    // User explicitly set CK as the flash attention backend. 397→\n   398→bool check_flash_causal_non_square_seqlens(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   399→  // FlashAttention 2 updated the default mask meaning for causal in this PR:\n   400→  // {\n   436→  const auto s_q = params.query.sym_size(2);\n   437→  const auto s_k = params.key.sym_size(2);\n   438→  const auto d_qk = params.query.sym_size(3);\n   439→  const auto d_v = 9.0.0\");\n   482→      }\n   483→      return false;\n   484→    }\n   485→    if (params.dropout != 0.0 && (s_q % 64 != 0 || s_k % 64 != 0)) {\n   486→      if (debug) {\n   487→ 493→  if (s_k == 1) {\n   494→    if (debug) {\n   495→      TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"cudnn SDPA does not support key/value sequence length 1.\");\n   496→    }\n   497→    return false;\n   498→  }\n   499→ return false;\n   504→  }\n   505→  return true;\n   506→}\n   507→\n   508→bool check_cudnn_layout(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n   509→  const int64_t h = params.query.size(1);\n   510→  const int64_t s_q = params.query.size(2);\n   511→  const int64_t d = params.query.size(3);\n   512→  const int64_t s_k = params.key.size(2);\n   513→  const int64_t s_v = params.value.size(2);\n   514→  // corresponds to cuDNN's \"packed QKV\" layout\n   515→  const bool packed_query_layout_ok = (params.query.stride(0) == s_q * 3 * h * d) &&\n   516→                                 (params.query.stride(1) == d) &&\n   517→                                 (params.query.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n   518→                                 (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n   519→  const bool packed_key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * 3 * h * d) &&\n   520→                               (params.key.stride(1) == d) &&\n   521→                               (params.key.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n   522→                               (params.key.stride(3) == 1);\n   523→  const bool packed_value_layout_ok = (params.value.stride(0) == s_v * 3 * h * d) &&\n   524→                                 (params.value.stride(1) == d) &&\n   525→                                 (params.value.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n   526→                                 (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n   527→\n   528→  const bool packed_layout_ok = packed_query_layout_ok && packed_key_layout_ok && packed_value_layout_ok;\n   529→\n   530→  const bool query_layout_ok = (params.query.stride(0) == s_q * h * d) &&\n   531→                               (params.query.stride(1) == d) &&\n   532→                               (params.query.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n   533→                               (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n   534→  const bool key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * h * d) &&\n   535→                              (params.key.stride(1) == d) &&\n   536→                              (params.key.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n   537→                              (params.key.stride(3) == 1);\n   538→  const bool value_layout_ok = (params.value.stride(0) == s_v * h * d) &&\n   539→                               (params.value.stride(1) == d) &&\n   540→                               (params.value.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n   541→                               (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n   542→\n   543→  const bool layout_ok = query_layout_ok && key_layout_ok && value_layout_ok;\n   544→\n   545→  if (!packed_value_layout_ok && !layout_ok) {\n   546→    if (debug) {\n   547→      if (!packed_layout_ok) {\n   548→        if (!packed_query_layout_ok) {\n   549→          TORCH_WARN(\"Query tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.query.strides());\n   550→        }\n   551→        if (!packed_key_layout_ok) {\n   552→          TORCH_WARN(\"Key tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.key.strides());\n   553→        }\n   554→        if (!packed_value_layout_ok) {\n   555→          TORCH_WARN(\"Value tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\",
